		<script type="text/javascript">
			$(document).ready(function(){
				//track event for showing popup
				_gaq.push(['_trackEvent', 'Popup', 'Subscribe', 'Show']);
				$('#newsletter-popup-container').delay(1000).fadeIn(800);
				$('#newscontainer').addClass('blur');
				
				$('.close-popup').click(function(e){
					e.preventDefault();
					//track event for closing popup
					_gaq.push(['_trackEvent', 'Popup', 'Subscribe', 'Close']);
					$('#newsletter-popup-container').fadeOut(800);
					$('#newscontainer').removeClass('blur');
				});
				
				$('#subscribe-form').submit(function(e){
					e.preventDefault();
					$('#newsletter-popup-container').slideUp(800, function(){
						$('#popup-content1').hide();
						$('#popup-content2').show();
						$('#newsletter-popup-container').slideDown(800);
						$.post("/ajax/subscribe_newsletter.php", { email: $("#email").val(), category: $("#subscribe_category").val(), slug: $("#subscribe_slug").val() }).done(function(data){
							$('#newsletter-popup-container').slideUp(800, function(){
								
								$('#popup-content2').hide();
								if(data == 'SUCCESS_EXISTING_USER' || data == 'SUCCESS_NEW_USER'){
									$('#popup-content3').show();								
									$('#newsletter-popup-container').slideDown(800).delay(1500).slideUp(800);
									$('#newscontainer').removeClass('blur');
									
									if(data == 'SUCCESS_EXISTING_USER'){
										//track event for subscribing by existing user
										_gaq.push(['_trackEvent', 'Popup', 'Subscribe', 'Added subscription (existing user)']);
									}else{
										//track event for subscribing by new user
										_gaq.push(['_trackEvent', 'Popup', 'Subscribe', 'Added subscription (new user)']);
									}
								}else{
									$('#email-error').show();
									$('#popup-content1').show();
									$('#newsletter-popup-container').slideDown(800);
								}
								
							});
						});
						
					});
				});
			});
		</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
	var categoryTimer;
	
	function hideCategories(){
		$(".active").removeClass("active");
		$(".open").slideUp(400);
	}
	
	$(document).ready(function(){
		$('.cat-navigation').hoverIntent(function(){
				$(".active").removeClass("active");
				$(this).addClass("active");
				
				toDisplay = '#cat-'+$(this).attr("id");
				$(".open").removeClass("open").slideUp(400,function(){
					$(toDisplay).slideDown(400);
					$(toDisplay).addClass("open");
				});
			},function(){
				//categoryTimer = setTimeout(hideCategories,500);
			}
		);	
		
				$('#country-flag').hoverIntent(
			function(){
				//$('#all-flags').slideDown(400);
				$('#country-flag').animate({width:'960px'},300);
			},
			function(){
				$('#country-flag').animate({width:'40px'},300);
			}
		);
				
		$('.homepagelinks').hover(function(){
			clearTimeout(categoryTimer);
		},function(){
			//hideCategories();
		});
		
	});
</script>
